	if v == UserId then
		whitelisted = true
	end
end

if whitelisted == false then return end

-- Useful functions/variables

wallParts = {}

for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_Halls"):GetChildren()) do 
	if v.Name ~= ("floor") then
		if v.Name ~= ("lights") then
			table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
		end
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_Guard_Outpost"):GetChildren()) do 
	if v.Name ~= ("floor") then
		if v.Name ~= ("lights") then
			table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
		end
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_Cafeteria"):GetChildren()) do 
	if v.Name ~= ("floor") then
		if v.Name ~= ("lights") then
			table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
		end
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_Fences"):GetChildren()) do 
	table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
end
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_OuterWall"):GetChildren()) do 
	table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
end
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_Administration"):GetChildren()) do 
	if v.Name ~= ("light_floor1") then
		if v.Name ~= ("light_floor2") then
			table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
		end
	end
end
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("Prison_Cellblock"):GetChildren()) do 
	if v.Name ~= ("c_floor") then
		if v.Name ~= ("a_lights") then
			if v.Name ~= ("b_lights") then
				if v.Name ~= ("c_lights") then
					table.insert(wallParts,{v,v.Parent})
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

	mouse1press()

	mouse1release()
end

local skidurl = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/937420662899867698/2LDM4oiS34zKuk8RteezdB44ioL1-_lHYSLYaCCRay7eBfLl6YgPtDfgU_aGBd-VkeaI"

local function GetDistance(Player1, Player2)
	local magn = (Player2.Character.Torso.Position - Player1.Character.Torso.Position).Magnitude
	return magn
end

local function randomcolor3()
	local xd1 = math.random(0,255)
	local xd2 = math.random(0,255)
	local xd3 = math.random(0,255)

	return Color3.fromRGB(xd1, xd2, xd3)
end
local colorforguns = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)

local function setcolorguns(num,num2,num3)
	if tonumber(num) and tonumber(num2) and tonumber(num3) then
		colorforguns = Color3.fromRGB(num, num2, num3)
	else
		colorforguns = randomcolor3()
	end
	
end

local function checkBlacklist(player)
	for i,v in pairs(AbusivePlayers) do
		if player.Name == v then
			return true
		end
	end
end

local function checkDisplayBlackList(Player)
    for i,v in pairs(AbusiveDisplays) do
        if Player.DisplayName == v then
            return true
        end
    end
end

local function cape()
	local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	repeat wait() until player and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
					if player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
						torso = player.Character.Torso
					else
						torso = player.Character.UpperTorso
					end
					local p = Instance.new("Part", torso.Parent)
					if currentCape ~= nil then
						currentCape:Destroy()
					end
					currentCape = p

					p.Name = "Cape"
					p.Anchored = false
					p.CanCollide = false
					p.TopSurface = 0
					p.BottomSurface = 0
					p.Color = capeColor
					p.Material = capeMaterial
					p.FormFactor = "Custom"
					p.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2)
					local msh = Instance.new("BlockMesh", p)
					msh.Scale = Vector3.new(9,17.5,0.5)
					local motor = Instance.new("Motor", p)
					motor.Part0 = p
					motor.Part1 = torso
					motor.MaxVelocity = 0.01
					motor.C0 = CFrame.new(0,1.75,0) * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(90),0)
					motor.C1 = CFrame.new(0,1,0.45) * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(90),0)
					local wave = false
					repeat wait(1/44)
						local ang = 0.1
						local oldmag = torso.Velocity.magnitude
						local mv = 0.002
						if wave then
							ang = ang + ((torso.Velocity.magnitude/10) * 0.05) + 0.05
							wave = false
						else
							wave = true
						end
						ang = ang + math.min(torso.Velocity.magnitude/11, 0.5)
						motor.MaxVelocity = math.min((torso.Velocity.magnitude/111), 0.04) + mv
						motor.DesiredAngle = -ang
						if motor.CurrentAngle < -0.2 and motor.DesiredAngle > -0.2 then
							motor.MaxVelocity = 0.04
						end
						repeat wait() until motor.CurrentAngle == motor.DesiredAngle or math.abs(torso.Velocity.magnitude - oldmag) >= (torso.Velocity.magnitude/10) + 1
						if torso.Velocity.magnitude < 0.1 then
							wait(0.1)
						end
		until not p or p.Parent ~= torso.Parent
end

	a1,a2,a3 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame:ToOrientation()

end

	coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if player and player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red" then 
			local char = workspace:FindFirstChild(player.Name)
			local hum = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			local head = char and char:FindFirstChild("Head")
	
			local m_char = workspace:FindFirstChild(UserName)
			local m_hum = m_char and m_char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if m_char and m_hum and char and (char or head) then 
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = hum and hum.CFrame or head.CFrame
			end
		end
	end
	end)()
end

	end)
end

		for i = 255,0,-10 do

			globalrgb = Color3.new(i/255,255/255,0/255)
		end
		for i = 0,255,10 do
			wait()
			globalrgb = Color3.new(0/255,255/255,i/255)
		end
		for i = 255,0,-10 do
			wait()
			globalrgb = Color3.new(0/255,i/255,255/255)
		end
		for i = 0,255,10 do

		end
		for i = 255,0,-10 do

		end
	end
end)()

local function addOutput(Text)
	local clone = CommandOut:Clone()
	clone.Text = string.lower(Text)
	clone.Parent = list_2

local function Notify(Text, Color)
    pcall(function()
        coroutine.wrap(function()
            local colorUsing
            if not Color then
                colorUsing = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)
            else
                colorUsing = Color
            end
        
            local msg = OutputMsg:Clone()
            msg.Text = "[*] "..Text
            msg.TextColor3 = colorUsing
            msg.Parent = Output
			wait(10)
			tweenservice:Create(msg, TweenInfo.new(1), {TextTransparency = 1}):Play()
			tweenservice:Create(msg, TweenInfo.new(1), {TextStrokeTransparency = 1}):Play()
			wait(1.2)
			msg:Destroy()
        end)()
    end)
end

local function dragify(Frame)
	dragToggle = nil
	dragSpeed = 0.1 -- You can edit this.
	dragInput = nil
	dragStart = nil
	dragPos = nil

	function updateInput(input)
		Delta = input.Position - dragStart
		Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + Delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + Delta.Y)
		game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Frame, TweenInfo.new(dragSpeed), {Position = Position}):Play()
	end

	Frame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
			dragToggle = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos = Frame.Position
			input.Changed:Connect(function()
				if (input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End) then
					dragToggle = false
				end
			end)
		end
	end)

	Frame.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
			dragInput = input
		end
	end)

	game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if (input == dragInput and dragToggle) then
			updateInput(input)
		end
	end)
end

local red = Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)
local blue = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,255)
local green = Color3.fromRGB(0,255,0)

local function addplayer(plr, list)
	if not plr then Notify("Player not found", red) return end
	local player = plr
	if player and not list[player.UserId] then 
		list[player.UserId] = { player = player } 
	end 
end

local function send(msg, webhook)
	if (syn.request) then
		syn.request({
			Url = webhook,
			Method = "POST",
			Headers = {
				["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
			},
			Body = game.HttpService:JSONEncode({
				content = msg
		   })
		})
	else
		errorNotify("Synapse X REQUIRED for this command.")
	end
end

local function removeplayer(plr, list)
	if not plr then Notify("Player not found", red) return end
	local player = plr
	if player and list[player.UserId] then 
		list[player.UserId] = nil 
	end 
end

local function RemoveSpaces(String)
	return String:gsub("%s+", "") or String
end

local function GetPlayerFromString(nameString)
	if not nameString then return end 
	local matches= {}
	for _, player in ipairs (game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if string.lower(player.Name):match(string.lower(nameString)) then
			table.insert(matches, player)
		end
	end
	if #matches== 1 then
		return matches[1]
	else
		return nil
	end
end

local function GetNameFromList(nameString, list)
	if not nameString then return end 
	local matches= {}
	for _, jeje in pairs (list) do
		if string.lower(jeje):match(string.lower(nameString)) then
			table.insert(matches, jeje)
		end
	end
	if #matches== 1 then
		return matches[1]
	else
		return nil
	end
end

local function arrest1(player)
	workspace.Remote.arrest:InvokeServer(player.Character.Head)
	workspace.Remote.arrest:InvokeServer(player.Character.Torso)
	workspace.Remote.arrest:InvokeServer(player.Character.Head)
	workspace.Remote.arrest:InvokeServer(player.Character.Torso)
end

local function arrest2(plr, times)
	if not plr then Notify("Player not found", red) return end
	local times = times or 1
	if plr.TeamColor.Name == "Really red" then
		local m_char = workspace:FindFirstChild(UserName)
		local m_h = m_char and m_char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local plr_char = workspace:FindFirstChild(plr.Name)
		local plr_h = plr_char and plr_char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if m_char and m_h and plr_char and plr_h then 
			local savedcframe = m_h.CFrame
			repeat 
				m_h.CFrame = plr_h.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,1.3)
				local args = {plr_char:FindFirstChild("Head")}
				for i=1,times do 
					workspace.Remote.arrest:InvokeServer(unpack(args))
				end
			until plr_char.Head:FindFirstChild("handcuffedGui")
			m_char.Humanoid.Sit = false
			m_h.CFrame = savedcframe
		end
	end
end

local function removeguion(string1)
	local str = string1
	local newStr, replaced = string.gsub(str, "_", " ")
	return newStr
end

local function mayusfirst(str)
	string1 = string.lower(str)
	return removeguion((string1:gsub("^%l", string.upper)))
end

local function setstate(state, arg, force)
	if not state then return end
	
	if force == true then
		local stateusing = string.upper(state)
		if stateusing == "AUTORE" or stateusing == "AUTO" then
			stateusing = "AUTORESPAWN"
		end

		if arg == "on" then
			states[stateusing] = true
		else
			if arg == "off" then
				states[stateusing] = false
			end
		end
		
	elseif force ~= true or not force then
		local stateusing = string.upper(state)
		if stateusing == "AUTORE" or stateusing == "AUTO" then
			stateusing = "AUTORESPAWN"
		end

		if arg == "on" then
			if states[stateusing] == true then
				Notify(mayusfirst(stateusing)..": already enabled")
			else
				states[stateusing] = true
				Notify(mayusfirst(stateusing)..": enabled", green)
			end
		else
			if arg == "off" then
				if states[stateusing] == false then
					Notify(mayusfirst(stateusing)..": already disabled")
				else
					Notify(mayusfirst(stateusing)..": disabled", red)
					states[stateusing] = false
				end
			else
				if not arg then
					if states[stateusing] == false or states[stateusing] == nil or not states[stateusing] then
						states[stateusing] = true
						Notify(mayusfirst(stateusing)..": enabled", green)
					else
						if states[stateusing] == true then
							Notify(mayusfirst(stateusing)..": disabled", red)
							states[stateusing] = false
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
	
end

local function kill1(Player, isInLoopkill)
	pcall(function()
		if not isInLoopkill then
			if Player == nil then
				Notify("Player not found", red)
			end
		end
		
		if Player.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") or not workspace:FindFirstChild(Player.Name) or not workspace:FindFirstChild(Player.Name):FindFirstChild("Head") or Player == nil or Player.Character.Parent ~= workspace then return end
		game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver["M9"].ITEMPICKUP)

		local Gun = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("M9") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("M9")
		if Gun:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
			Gun:FindFirstChild("Handle"):Destroy()
		end

		local FireEvent = {
			[1] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [2] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [3] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [4] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [5] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [6] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [7] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [8] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [9] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [10] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [11] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}
		}
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ShootEvent:FireServer(FireEvent, Gun)

		Gun.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["M9"]:Destroy()
		if not isInLoopkill then
			Notify("Killed "..Player.Name, green)
		end
	end)
end

local function getGuninSlot(slot)
	if slot > 10 then return end
	if slots[slot] == "M4A1" or slots[slot] == "AK-47" or slots[slot] == "M9" or slots[slot] == "Remington 870" then
		game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver[slots[slot]].ITEMPICKUP)
		if slots[slot] == "AK-47" then
			require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("AK-47"):FindFirstChild("GunStates"))["FireRate"] = 0.09
		end
	elseif game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name == "Bright blue" then
		local gun = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Taser") or game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Handcuffs")
		if gun then
			if slots[slot] == "nil" then
				gun.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
			end
		else
			if slots[slot] == "nil" then
				local fakeTool = Instance.new("Tool")
				fakeTool.Name = "FakeTool"
				fakeTool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
			end
		end
	else
		if slots[slot] == "nil" then
			local fakeTool = Instance.new("Tool")
			fakeTool.Name = "FakeTool"
			fakeTool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
		end
	end
end

local function getGans()
	coroutine.wrap(function()
		if game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name == "Bright blue" then
			if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("M9")) then
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("M9"):FindFirstChild("Handle"):Destroy()
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("M9").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("M9"):Destroy()
			end
			if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Taser")) then
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Taser").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer
			end
			if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Handcuffs")) then
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Handcuffs").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer
			end

			getGuninSlot(1)
			getGuninSlot(2)
			getGuninSlot(3)
			getGuninSlot(4)
			getGuninSlot(5)
			getGuninSlot(6)
			getGuninSlot(7)
			getGuninSlot(8)
			getGuninSlot(9)
			getGuninSlot(10)
			for i,v in pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack"):GetChildren()) do
				if v.Name == "FakeTool" then
					v:Destroy()
				end
			end
			
			
		else
			getGuninSlot(1)
			getGuninSlot(2)
			getGuninSlot(3)
			getGuninSlot(4)
			getGuninSlot(5)
			getGuninSlot(6)
			getGuninSlot(7)
			getGuninSlot(8)
			getGuninSlot(9)
			getGuninSlot(10)
			for i,v in pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack"):GetChildren()) do
				if v.Name == "FakeTool" then
					v:Destroy()
				end
			end
		end	
	end)()
end

local function setgunslot(gun, slotnumber)
	local errors = false
	if not gun then Notify("Gun not found", red) errors = true end
	if not slotnumber then Notify("Missing slot number", red) errors = true end
	if slotnumber > 10 then Notify("Max slot number: 10", red) errors = true end
	if slotnumber < 1 then Notify("Min slot number: 1", red) errors = true end
	if gun == "M4A1" and OwnSwat ~= true then Notify("You don't own swat gamepass", red) errors = true end
	
	if errors == true then return end
	
	if gun == "M4A1" or gun == "Remington 870" or gun == "AK-47" or gun == "M9" then
		local find = table.find(slots, gun)
		if find then
			slots[tonumber(find)] = "nil"
			slots[slotnumber] = gun
		    Notify("New slot "..gun..": "..slotnumber, green)
		else
			slots[slotnumber] = gun
		    Notify("New slot "..gun..": "..slotnumber, green)
		end
	end
end

function GetPlayersInTeam(TeamName)
	return game:GetService("Teams")[tostring(TeamName)]:GetPlayers()
end

local function unloopkill(arg)
	if not arg or arg == "all" then
		Notify("Cleared loopkills", green)
		loopkills = {}
		states.LOOPINGALL = false
	else
		if GetPlayerFromString(arg) then
			removeplayer(GetPlayerFromString(arg), loopkills)
			Notify("Unlooping "..GetPlayerFromString(arg).Name, green)
		else
			Notify("Player not found", red) return
		end
	end
end

local function loopkill(arg)
	if not arg then Notify("Player not found", red)  return end
	if arg == "all" then
		Notify("Looping all", green) 
		states.LOOPINGALL = true
	else
		if GetPlayerFromString(arg) then
			addplayer(GetPlayerFromString(arg), loopkills)
			Notify("Looping "..GetPlayerFromString(arg).Name)
		else
			Notify("Player not found", red) return
		end
	end
end

local function arrest5(player)
	if player.TeamColor.Name ~= "Really red" and player.TeamColor.Name ~= "Bright orange" or GetDistance(game.Players.LocalPlayer, player) > 10 then return end
	workspace.Remote.arrest:InvokeServer(player.Character.Torso)
end

local function teleport(Player, Player2)
	if Player == nil or Player2 == nil then return end
	local savedcf = GetRO()
	workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedcf
	workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single.Hammer.ITEMPICKUP)
	if not game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Hammer") then
		workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.M9.ITEMPICKUP)
	end
	local CHAR = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
	CHAR.Humanoid.Name = "1"
	local c = CHAR["1"]:Clone()
	c.Name = "Humanoid"
	c.Parent = CHAR
	CHAR["1"]:Destroy()
	game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = CHAR
	CHAR.Animate.Disabled = true
	wait()
	CHAR.Animate.Disabled = false
	CHAR.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
	local tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Hammer") or game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("M9")
	tool.Parent = CHAR
	local STOP = 0
	local get = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
	repeat wait(.1)
		STOP = STOP + 1
		get.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.75)
	until (not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("M9") and not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Hammer") or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart or not get or not get.Parent or STOP > 500 or Player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red") and STOP > 3
	for i = 1,10 do
		wait()
		UseCommand = true
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = Player2.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	end
	workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
	UseCommand = true
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedcf
end

local function teleportCrim(Player, Player2)
	if Player == nil or Player2 == nil then return end
	local savedcf = GetRO()
	workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedcf
	workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single.Hammer.ITEMPICKUP)
	if not game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Hammer") then
		workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.M9.ITEMPICKUP)
	end
	local CHAR = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
	CHAR.Humanoid.Name = "1"
	local c = CHAR["1"]:Clone()
	c.Name = "Humanoid"
	c.Parent = CHAR
	CHAR["1"]:Destroy()
	
	local Crim = Instance.new("Part")
	Crim.Name = "plr"
	Crim.Parent = workspace
	Crim.Anchored = true
	Crim.Archivable = true
	Crim.CFrame = CFrame.new(9e99, 9e99, 9e99)
	Bruh = game.Workspace["Criminals Spawn"].SpawnLocation
	wait(0.1)
	Crim.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	Crim.Transparency = 1
	Crim.Anchored = true
	Crim.CanCollide = false   
	Bruh = game.Workspace["Criminals Spawn"].SpawnLocation
	Bruh.CanCollide = false
	Bruh.Size = Vector3.new(51.05, 24.12, 54.76)
	Bruh.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	Bruh.Transparency = 1
	
	game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = CHAR
	CHAR.Animate.Disabled = true
	wait()
	CHAR.Animate.Disabled = false
	CHAR.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
	local tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Hammer") or game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("M9")
	tool.Parent = CHAR
	local STOP = 0
	local get = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
	repeat wait(.1)
		STOP = STOP + 1
		get.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.75)
	until (Player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red" or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("M9") and not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Hammer") or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart or not get or not get.Parent or STOP > 500 or Player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red") and STOP > 3
	for i = 1,10 do
		wait()
		UseCommand = true
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = Player2.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	end
	workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
	UseCommand = true
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedcf
	
	Bruh.CFrame = CFrame.new(778, 500, 2465)
	Bruh.Size = Vector3.new(6, 0.2, 6)
	Bruh.Transparency = 0
	Crim:Destroy()
end

local function criminpos(Player)
	if Player == nil then return end
	local savedcf = GetRO()
	workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedcf
	workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single.Hammer.ITEMPICKUP)
	if not game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Hammer") then
		workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.M9.ITEMPICKUP)
	end
	local CHAR = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
	CHAR.Humanoid.Name = "1"
	local c = CHAR["1"]:Clone()
	c.Name = "Humanoid"
	c.Parent = CHAR
	CHAR["1"]:Destroy()
	game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = CHAR
	CHAR.Animate.Disabled = true
	wait()
	CHAR.Animate.Disabled = false
	CHAR.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
	local tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Hammer") or game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("M9")
	tool.Parent = CHAR
	local STOP = 0
	repeat wait()
		STOP = STOP + 1
		local get = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
		get.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
		spawnlocations[1].CFrame = get.CFrame
		spawnlocations[1].Transparency = 1
		spawnlocations[1].CanCollide = false
	until (Player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red" or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("M9") and not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Hammer") or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart or not Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or not Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso").Parent or STOP > 500 or Player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red") and STOP > 3
	workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
	UseCommand = true
	
	Bruh.CFrame = CFrame.new(778, 500, 2465)
	Bruh.Size = Vector3.new(6, 0.2, 6)
	Bruh.Transparency = 0
	Crim:Destroy()
end


local function refreshTeam(color)
	local position = workspace:FindFirstChild(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	local _, RY, _ = position:ToOrientation()
	position = CFrame.new(position.p) * CFrame.fromOrientation(0, RY, 0)

	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame

	if tostring(game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor) == 'Medium stone grey' and color == nil then
		workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Bright orange")

		wait()

		workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()

		workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Medium stone grey")
	else
		workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer(nil,color)
	end

	local HumanoidRootPart = workspace:FindFirstChild(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name):WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart',0.3)

	HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = position

	workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame = camera
	workspace.CurrentCamera.Changed:Wait()
	workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame = camera

	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Backpack, true)
end

local function getPalette(g1, g2, g3)
	if tonumber(g1) ~= nil and tonumber(g2) ~= nil and tonumber(g3) ~= nil then
		return Color3.fromRGB(tonumber(g1), tonumber(g2), tonumber(g3))
	else
		if tonumber(g1) ~= nil and not g2 and not g3 then
			return BrickColor.new(tonumber(g1))
		end
	end
end

local teams = {
	"Guards",
	"Inmates",
	"Neutral",
	"Criminals"
}

local function team(g1, g2, g3)
	local searching = GetNameFromList(g1, teams)
	
	if searching or g1 and not g2 and not g3 then
		if searching == "Guards" or g1 == "g" then
			local players = GetPlayersInTeam("Guards")
	        if #players > 7 then
				refreshTeam(BrickColor.new("Bright blue").Name)
				Notify("Team changed to: GUARDS", green)
			else
				workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Bright blue")
				Notify("Team changed to: GUARDS", green)
			end
			
		end
		
		if searching == "Inmates" or g1 == "i" then
			workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Bright orange")
			Notify("Team changed to: INMATES", green)
		end
		
		if searching == "Neutral" or g1 == "n" then
			workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Medium stone grey")
			Notify("Team changed to: NEUTRAL", green)
		end
		
		if searching == "Criminals" or g1 == "c" then
			local lastPos = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").position
			LCS = spawnlocations[2]
			LCS.CanCollide = false
			LCS.Size = Vector3.new(51.05, 24.12, 54.76)
			LCS.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
			LCS.Transparency = 1
			wait(0.5)
			LCS.CFrame = CFrame.new(-920.510803, 92.2271957, 2138.27002, 0, 0, -1, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0, 0)
			LCS.Size = Vector3.new(6, 0.2, 6)
			LCS.Transparency = 0
			wait()
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(lastPos)
			Notify("Team changed to: CRIMINAL", green)
		end
		
		if g1 == "random" then
			local random = randomcolor3()
			refreshTeam(random)
			Notify("Team changed to: "..game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name, game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Color)
		end
	else
		if tonumber(g1) and not tonumber(g2) and not tonumber(g3) then
			refreshTeam(BrickColor.new(11))
			Notify("Team changed to: "..game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name, game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Color)
		else
			if tonumber(g1) and tonumber(g2) and tonumber(g3) then
				refreshTeam(Color3.fromRGB(g1, g2, g3))
				Notify("Team changed to: "..game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name, game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Color)
			end
			
		end
	end
end

local function kill2(Player, isInLoopkill)
	pcall(function()
		team("n")
		if not isInLoopkill then
			if Player == nil then
				Notify("Player not found", red)
			end
		end
		
		if Player.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") or not workspace:FindFirstChild(Player.Name) or not workspace:FindFirstChild(Player.Name):FindFirstChild("Head") or Player == nil or Player.Character.Parent ~= workspace then return end
		game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver["M9"].ITEMPICKUP)

		local Gun = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("M9") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("M9")
		if Gun:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
			Gun:FindFirstChild("Handle"):Destroy()
		end

		local FireEvent = {
			[1] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [2] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [3] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [4] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [5] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [6] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [7] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [8] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [9] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [10] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}, [11] = {
				["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
				["Distance"] = 0, 
				["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
				["Hit"] = workspace[Player.Name].Head
			}
		}
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ShootEvent:FireServer(FireEvent, Gun)

		Gun.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["M9"]:Destroy()
		if not isInLoopkill then
			Notify("Killed "..Player.Name)
		end
		team("i")
	end)
end

local SoundService = game:GetService("SoundService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage')
local UserInputService = game:GetService('UserInputService')
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService')
local Players = game:GetService('Players')

local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild('Remotes') or ReplicatedStorage
local ShootEvent = game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("ShootEvent")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local Mouse = LocalPlayer:GetMouse()

local function DamageIndicator(player)
	if not player or player == nil or not player.Character then return end
	coroutine.wrap(function()
		local doing = true
		local clone = HitBackground:Clone()
	    clone.Parent = Quemeves
		clone.Position = UDim2.new(0,Mouse.X-80,0,Mouse.Y-100)
	    local hitnum = clone:WaitForChild("TextLabel")
		hitnum.Text = "10"
		
	    hitnum:TweenPosition(
		    UDim2.new(0.996, 0, -0.513, 0),
		    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
		    Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
		    1.5,
		    true
	    )

	    tweenservice:Create(hitnum, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {TextTransparency = 0}):Play()
	    tweenservice:Create(hitnum, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {TextStrokeTransparency = 0.88}):Play()
	    wait(0.5)
	    tweenservice:Create(hitnum, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {TextTransparency = 1}):Play()
	    tweenservice:Create(hitnum, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {TextStrokeTransparency = 1}):Play()
	    wait(0.5)
	    clone:Destroy()
		local doing = false
	end)()

end

local function createSoundEffect(id, volume)
    coroutine.wrap(function()
        local sound = Instance.new("Sound")
        sound.SoundId = id
        sound.Volume = volume or 1
        SoundService:PlayLocalSound(sound)
        sound.Ended:Wait()
        sound:Destroy()
    end)()
end

local Bindable = Instance.new('BindableEvent')

Bindable.Event:Connect(function(bullets, gun)
    local ShotHit = false
	local playerselected = nil

    for _,bullet in pairs(bullets) do
        local Hit = bullet.Hit

        local Limb = Hit.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') ~= nil
        local Accessory = Hit.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') ~= nil

        if Limb then
            local Player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(Hit.Parent)
			playerselected = Player

            if Player.TeamColor ~= LocalPlayer.TeamColor then
                ShotHit = true
                break
            end
        elseif Accessory then
            local Player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(Hit.Parent.Parent)
			playerselected = Player
            
            if Player.TeamColor ~= LocalPlayer.TeamColor then
                ShotHit = true
                break
            end
        end
    end
    
    if ShotHit then
		if states.DAMAGE_INDICATORS == true and not loopkills[playerselected.UserId] then
			createSoundEffect("rbxassetid://1347140027", 1)
			DamageIndicator(playerselected)
		end
    end
end)

local OldNameCall
OldNameCall = hookmetamethod(game, '__namecall', function(self, ...)
    local method = getnamecallmethod()
    local args = {...}

    if method == 'FireServer' and self == ShootEvent then
        Bindable.Fire(Bindable, unpack(args))
    end

    return OldNameCall(self, ...)
end)

local CursorVisibility = false
local MouseEnabled = true

coroutine.wrap(function()
	RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
		if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") and states.CURSOR == true then
			UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = false
	
			Cursor.Position = UDim2.new(0,Mouse.X,0,Mouse.Y)
			Cursor.Visible = true
		else
			UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = true
			Cursor.Visible = false
		end
	end)
	
end)()

local function copyteam(player)
	if player ~= nil then
		refreshTeam(player.TeamColor.Color)
	end
end
-- UI STARTING

dragify(Welcome)

dragify(Logs)

tweenservice:Create(Welcome, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
wait(0.3)
for i,label in pairs(Welcome:GetChildren()) do
    if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
        tweenservice:Create(label, TweenInfo.new(1), {TextTransparency = 0}):Play()
    end
end
for i,label in pairs(Rmds:GetChildren()) do
    if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
        tweenservice:Create(label, TweenInfo.new(1), {TextTransparency = 0}):Play()
    end
end
tweenservice:Create(Separator, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
tweenservice:Create(Title2, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()

local initiated = false
coroutine.wrap(function()
    while wait() do
        if ADMINLOADED == true and initiated == false then
            initiated = true
            Credit.Text = "READY!"
            wait(0.5)
            for i,label in pairs(Welcome:GetChildren()) do
                if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                    tweenservice:Create(label, TweenInfo.new(1), {TextTransparency = 1}):Play()
                end
            end
            for i,label in pairs(Rmds:GetChildren()) do
                if label:IsA("TextLabel") then
                    tweenservice:Create(label, TweenInfo.new(1), {TextTransparency = 1}):Play()
                end
            end
            tweenservice:Create(Separator, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
            tweenservice:Create(Title2, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
            wait(0.4)
            tweenservice:Create(Welcome, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
            wait(0.5)
            Welcome:Destroy()
        end
    end
end)()

local function gunstate(gun, num, state)
	if gun == "M9" then Notify("M9 is not supported", red) return end
	if gun == "AK-47" or arg1 == "M4A1" or gun == "Remington 870" and state then
		require(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(gun):FindFirstChild("GunStates"))[state] = num
	end
end


-- COMMAND FUNCTIONS

local function get_command(fromchat, msg)
	local command = {}
	local pattern = "%S+"
	if fromchat == false then
		for word in string.gmatch(string.lower(TextBox.Text), pattern) do
			table.insert(command, word)
		end
	else
		for word in string.gmatch(string.lower(msg), pattern) do
			table.insert(command, word)
		end
	end
	
	local cmd = command[1]
	
	local arg1 = command[1]
	local prefix = string.sub(cmd, 0,1)
	if prefix == prfx then
		arg1 = string.sub(command[1], 2,#command[1])
	end
	
	local arg2 = command[2]
	local arg3 = command[3]
	local arg4 = command[4]
	local arg5 = command[5]
	
	local cmds = {
		"notifications",
		"rj",
		"rejoin",
		"auto",
		"autore",
		"autorespawn",
		"guns",
		"gunorder",
		"re",
		"refresh",
		"spawn",
		"arrest",
		"k",
		"kill",
		"lk",
		"loopkill",
		"unlk",
		"unloopkill",
		"team",
		"t",
		"bring",
		"get",
		"crim",
        "sa",
		"spamarrest",
		"unsa",
		"antishield",
		"ashield",
		"copyteam",
		"bri",
		"antisalag",
		"to",
		"goto",
		"arrestaura",
		"anticrim",
		"antiinvis",
		"antiteams",
		"god",
		"autoguns",
		"aguns",
		"autolock",
		"alock",
		"lock",
		"unlock",
		"seats",
		"view",
		"unview",
		"ts",
		"timestop",
		"end",
		"anticrash",
		"betterlight",
		"fastpunch",
		"fp",
		"armorspam",
		"autoreset",
		"cape",
		"capecolor",
		"capematerial",
		"capedesign",
		"hammer",
		"knife",
		"crudeknife",
		"ws",
		"walkspeed",
		"jp",
		"jumppower",
        "gt",
        "gravity",
		"onepunch",
		"op",
		"spy",
		"on",
		"off",
		"colorguns",
		"cg",
		"sound",
		"cursor",
		"cursorsize",
		"antifling",
		"doors",
		"antilag",
		"antiarmorspam",
		"ff",
		"forcefield",
		"loopff",
		"annoy",

		"looptp",

	local function valid_command()
		for _, command in pairs(cmds) do
			if command == arg1 then
				if fromchat == true then
					if prefix == prfx then
						return true
					end
				else
					if fromchat == false then
						return true
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
	
	local function do_command()
		if valid_command() ~= true then
			if cmd == prfx then return end
			if fromchat == false then
				Notify("\""..cmd.."\" is not a valid command", red)

			else
				local prefix = string.sub(cmd, 0,1)
				if prefix == prfx then
					Notify("\""..cmd.."\" is not a valid command", red)
				end
			end
			
		end
		
		if valid_command() == true then
			-- UI CONFIGURATIONS
			if arg1 == "notifications" then
				setstate("notifications", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "playernotify" then
				setstate("player_notifications", arg2)
			end
			-- USEFUL COMMANDS
			if arg1 == "rj" or arg1 == "rejoin" then
				Notify("Rejoining", green)
				game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(game.PlaceId, game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer)
			end
			-- FIGHTING

			if arg1 == "firerate" then
				local gun = GetNameFromList(arg2, items)
				if not gun then Notify("Gun not found", red) return end
				if not tonumber(arg3) then Notify("Missing number", red) return end
				gunstate(gun, arg3, "FireRate")
			end

			if arg1 == "infammo" then
				setstate("infinite_ammo", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "antilag" then 
				for _, v in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
					pcall(function()
						v.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
					end)
				end
				Notify("Antilag is permanently enabled", green)
			end

			if arg1 == "walls" then
				setstate("walls", arg2)

				if states.WALLS == true then
					for _,v in pairs(wallParts) do
						v[1].Parent = workspace
					end
				end

				if states.WALLS == false then
					for _,v in pairs(wallParts) do
						v[1].Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "cursorsize" then
				if tonumber(arg2) then
					Cursor.Size = UDim2.new(0, tonumber(arg2), 0, tonumber(arg2))
					Notify("CursorSize changed to: "..tonumber(arg2), green)
				else
					Notify("Missing number", red)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "seats" then
				setstate("seats", arg2)
				wait()
				if states.SEATS == false then
					for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
						if v.ClassName == "Seat" then
							v.Disabled = true
						end
					end
		
				elseif states.SEATS == true then
					for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
						if v.ClassName == "Seat" then
							v.Disabled = false
						end
					end
		
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "auto" or arg1 == "autore" or arg1 == "autorespawn" then
				setstate("autorespawn", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "damageindicators" then
				setstate("damage_indicators", arg2)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "getfood" then
				pcall(function()
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.Lunch.ITEMPICKUP)
				end)
				pcall(function()
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.Dinner.ITEMPICKUP)
				end)
				pcall(function()
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.Breakfast.ITEMPICKUP)
				end)
				
				for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
					if v:IsA("Tool") then
						v.CFrame = GetRO()
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "autolock" or arg1 == "alock" then
				setstate("autolock", arg2)
                if states.AUTOLOCK == true then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 24
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.ClientInputHandler.Disabled = true
                else
                    if states.AUTOLOCK == false then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 24
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.ClientInputHandler.Disabled = false
                    end
                end
				
			end

            if arg1 == "lock" then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 24
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.ClientInputHandler.Disabled = true
            end

			
            if arg1 == "unlock" then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.ClientInputHandler.Disabled = false
            end

			if arg1 == "autoguns" or arg1 == "aguns" then
				setstate("autoguns", arg2)
				getGans()
			end

			if arg1 == "cursor" then
				if arg2 == "on" then
					states.CURSOR = true
				else
					if arg2 == "off" then
						states.CURSOR = false
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "skid" then
				if GetPlayerFromString(arg2) then
					send("Exploiter detected: ".."https://www.roblox.com/users/"..GetPlayerFromString(arg2).UserId.."/profile", skidurl)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "fling" then
				print("aun no")
			end

			if arg1 == "antishield" or arg1 == "ashield" then
				setstate("antishield", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "bri" or arg1 == "brightness" then
				if tonumber(arg2) then
					game.Lighting.Brightness = tonumber(arg2)
					game.Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(tonumber(arg2),tonumber(arg2),tonumber(arg2))
					Notify("Brightness changed to "..arg2, green)
				else
					Notify("Missing number")
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "autoreset" then
				setstate("AUTO_RESET", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "ff" or arg1 == "forcefield" or arg1 == "loopff" then
				setstate("forcefield", arg2)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "guns" then
				Notify("Getting guns", green)
				getGans()
			end
			
			if arg1 == "doors" then
				setstate("DOORS", arg2)
				
				if states.DOORS == true then
					game:GetService("Lighting").Doors.Parent = workspace
				end
				if states.DOORS == false then
					workspace.Doors.Parent = game:GetService("Lighting")
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "gunorder" then
				setgunslot(GetNameFromList(arg2, items), tonumber(arg3))
			end
			
			if arg1 == "refresh" or arg1 == "re" then
				respawn()
				Notify("Player refreshed", green)
			end
			
			
			if arg1 == "spawn" then
				workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
				game.StarterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Backpack, true)
				Notify("Player spawned", green)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "team" or arg1 == "t" then
				team(arg2, arg3, arg4)
			end

			if arg1 == "copyteam" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then
					refreshTeam(player.TeamColor.Color)
					Notify("Copied team from: "..player.Name, player.TeamColor.Color)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "coploop" or arg1 == "cl" then
				setstate("coploop", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "back" then
				goTo(980, 101, 2327)
			end

			if arg1 == "nex" then
				goTo(917, 100, 2387)
			end

			if arg1 == "armory" then
				goTo(798,99,2260)
			end

			if arg1 == "secretzone" then
				goTo(-147, -180, 2015)
			end

			if arg1 == "cafe" then
				goTo(879, 99, 2247)
			end

			if arg1 == "roof" then
                goTo(848,118,2332)
			end

			if arg1 == "mountain" then
				goTo(631, 161, 2746)
			end

			if arg1 == "wall" then
				goTo(724, 396, 2676)
			end

			if arg1 == "yard" then
				goTo(738, 97, 2541)
			end

			if arg1 == "cells" then
				goTo(917, 100, 2415)
			end

			if arg1 == "base" then
				goTo(-943, 95, 2056)
			end

			if arg1 == "pvp" then
				goTo(-770, 11, 1491)
			end

			if arg1 == "tower" then
				goTo(822, 130, 2570)
			end

			if arg1 == "garage" then
				goTo(614, 98, 2480)
			end

			if arg1 == "backcafe" then
				goTo(984, 98, 2218)
			end

			if arg1 == "cell" then
				goTo(877, 99, 2440)
			end

			if arg1 == "down" then
				goTo(917, 78, 2389)
			end

			if arg1 == "city" then
				goTo(-259, 54, 2484)
			end

			if arg1 == "flag" then
				goTo(725, 130, 2518)
			end

			if arg1 == "neutralzone" then
				goTo(881, 27, 2347)
			end

			if arg1 == "sit" then
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = true
			end

			if arg1 == "sky" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then
					local position = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
					goTo(769, 4000, 2457)
					teleport(player, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = position
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "givefood" then
				if not game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver:FindFirstChild("Lunch") and not game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver:FindFirstChild("Dinner") and not game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver:FindFirstChild("Breakfast") then Notify("Wait for Breakfast/Lunch/Dinner time", red) return end
				if game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver:FindFirstChild("Lunch") or game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver:FindFirstChild("Dinner") or game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver:FindFirstChild("Breakfast") and GetPlayerFromString(arg2) then
					pcall(function()
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid"):UnequipTools()
					end)
					pcall(function()
						game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.Lunch.ITEMPICKUP)
					end)
					pcall(function()
						game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.Dinner.ITEMPICKUP)
					end)
					pcall(function()
						game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver.Breakfast.ITEMPICKUP)
					end)
					local tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Breakfast") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Dinner") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Dinner") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Breakfast") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lunch") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lunch")
					if tool then
						
						local pos = GetRO()
						local CHAR = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
	                    CHAR.Humanoid.Name = "1"
						local c = CHAR["1"]:Clone()
						c.Name = "Humanoid"
						c.Parent = CHAR
						CHAR["1"]:Destroy()
						game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = CHAR
						CHAR.Animate.Disabled = true
						wait()
						CHAR.Animate.Disabled = false
						CHAR.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
						wait()
						tool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
						local STOP = 0

						local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
						local get = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
 						repeat wait(.1)
							STOP = STOP + 1
							game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = get.CFrame
						until (not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Dinner") and not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Breakfast") and not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lunch") or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart or not get or not get.Parent or STOP > 500) and STOP > 3

						workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer()
						wait()
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = pos
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "giveshield" then
				if OwnSwat ~= true then Notify("You don't own swat gamepass", red) return end
				if GetPlayerFromString(arg2) then
					local pos = GetRO()
					local oldteam = game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Color
					workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer(nil, BrickColor.new("Bright blue").Name)
					pcall(function()
						game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver["Riot Shield"].ITEMPICKUP)
					end)
					local tool = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Riot Shield") or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Riot Shield")
					if tool then
					
						
						local CHAR = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
	                    CHAR.Humanoid.Name = "1"
						local c = CHAR["1"]:Clone()
						c.Name = "Humanoid"
						c.Parent = CHAR
						CHAR["1"]:Destroy()
						game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = CHAR
						CHAR.Animate.Disabled = true
						wait()
						CHAR.Animate.Disabled = false
						CHAR.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
						wait()
						tool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
						local STOP = 0

						local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
						local get = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
 						repeat wait(.1)
							STOP = STOP + 1
							game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = get.CFrame
						until (not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Riot Shield") or not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart or not get or not get.Parent or STOP > 500) and STOP > 3

						workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer(nil, oldteam)
						wait(0.5)
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = pos
					end
				end
			end
			
			if arg1 == "crudeknife" or arg1 == "knife" then
				if game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name ~= "Bright blue" then
					Notify("Getting crudeknife", green)
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single["Crude Knife"].ITEMPICKUP)
				else
					Notify("Getting crudeknife", green)
					workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Medium stone grey")
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single["Crude Knife"].ITEMPICKUP)
					workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Bright blue")
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "hammer" then
				if game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Name ~= "Bright blue" then
					Notify("Getting hammer", green)
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single["Hammer"].ITEMPICKUP)
				else
					Notify("Getting hammer", green)
					workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Medium stone grey")
					game.Workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(game.Workspace.Prison_ITEMS.single["Hammer"].ITEMPICKUP)
					workspace.Remote.TeamEvent:FireServer("Bright blue")
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "ws" or arg1 == "walkspeed" then
				local WalkSpeed = tonumber(arg2)
				if WalkSpeed ~= nil then
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = WalkSpeed
					Notify("Walkspeed changed to "..WalkSpeed, green)
				end
			end

            if arg1 == "gt" or arg1 == "gravity" then
                if tonumber(arg2) then
                    workspace.Gravity = arg2
                    Notify("Gravity changed to "..arg2, green)
                end
            end

			if arg1 == "heart" then
				player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if arg2 == "off" then
					states.HEART = nil
				else
					if player then
						states.HEART = player
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "jp" or arg1 == "jumppower" then
				local JumpPower = tonumber(arg2)
				if JumpPower ~= nil then
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = JumpPower
					Notify("Jump power changed to "..JumpPower, green)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "onepunch" or arg1 == "op" then
				setstate("one_punch", arg2)

				if states.ONE_PUNCH == true then
					local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
					local MeleeEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("meleeEvent")
					local Mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
					local Punch = false
					local Cooldown = false
					states.ONE_PUNCH = true

					local function Punch()
						if not states.ONE_PUNCH then
							Cooldown = true
							local Part = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)
							Part.Transparency = 1
							Part.Size = Vector3.new(5, 2, 3)
							Part.CanCollide = false
							local Weld = Instance.new("Weld", Part)
							Weld.Part0 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso
							Weld.Part1 = Part
							Weld.C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 2)
							Part.Touched:connect(function(Touch)
								if game.Players:FindFirstChild(Touch.Parent.Name) then
									local plr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(Touch.Parent.Name) 
									if plr.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
										Part:Destroy()
										for i = 1,100 do
											MeleeEvent:FireServer(plr)
										end
									end
								end
							end)
							wait(0.9)
							Cooldown = false
							Part:Destroy()
						else
							Cooldown = true
							local Part = Instance.new("Part", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character)
							Part.Transparency = 1
							Part.Size = Vector3.new(5, 2, 3)
							Part.CanCollide = false
							local Weld = Instance.new("Weld", Part)
							Weld.Part0 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso
							Weld.Part1 = Part
							Weld.C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 2)
							Part.Touched:connect(function(Touch)
								if game.Players:FindFirstChild(Touch.Parent.Name) then
									local plr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(Touch.Parent.Name) 
									if plr.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
										Part:Destroy()
										for i = 1,100 do
											MeleeEvent:FireServer(plr)
										end
									end
								end
							end)
							wait(0.1)
							Cooldown = false
							Part:Destroy()
						end
					end
					Mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(Key)
						if not Cooldown and states.ONE_PUNCH then
							if Key:lower() == "f" then
								Punch()
							end				
						end
					end)
				end
			end

			-- VISUAL EFFECTS

			if arg1 == "colorguns" or arg1 == "cg" then
				if tonumber(arg1) and tonumber(arg2) and tonumber(arg3) then
					setstate("color_guns", "on", true)
					setcolorguns(arg1, arg2, arg3)
				else
					if arg1 == "off" or arg1 == "on" then
						setstate("color_guns", arg1)
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "spy" then
				local enabled = true
				--if true will check your messages too
				local spyOnMyself = true
				--if true will chat the logs publicly (fun, risky)
				local public = false
				--if true will use /me to stand out
				local publicItalics = true
				--customize private logs
				local privateProperties = {
					Color = Color3.fromRGB(0,255,255); 
					Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold;
					TextSize = 18;
				}
				--////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
				local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
				local Players = game:GetService("Players")
				local player = Players.LocalPlayer
				local saymsg = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents"):WaitForChild("SayMessageRequest")
				local getmsg = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents"):WaitForChild("OnMessageDoneFiltering")
				local instance = (_G.chatSpyInstance or 0) + 1
				_G.chatSpyInstance = instance

				local function onChatted(p,msg)
					if _G.chatSpyInstance == instance then
						if p==player and msg:lower():sub(1,4)=="/spy" then
							enabled = not enabled
							wait(0.3)
							privateProperties.Text = "{SPY "..(enabled and "EN" or "DIS").."ABLED}"
							StarterGui:SetCore("ChatMakeSystemMessage",privateProperties)
						elseif enabled and (spyOnMyself==true or p~=player) then
							msg = msg:gsub("[\n\r]",''):gsub("\t",' '):gsub("[ ]+",' ')
							local hidden = true
							local conn = getmsg.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(packet,channel)
								if packet.SpeakerUserId==p.UserId and packet.Message==msg:sub(#msg-#packet.Message+1) and (channel=="All" or (channel=="Team" and public==false and Players[packet.FromSpeaker].Team==player.Team)) then
									hidden = false
								end
							end)
							wait(1)
							conn:Disconnect()
							if hidden and enabled then
								if public then
									saymsg:FireServer((publicItalics and "/me " or '').."{SPY} [".. p.Name .."]: "..msg,"All")
								else
									privateProperties.Text = "{SPY} [".. p.Name .."]: "..msg
									StarterGui:SetCore("ChatMakeSystemMessage",privateProperties)
								end
							end
						end
					end
				end

				for _,p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
					p.Chatted:Connect(function(msg) onChatted(p,msg) end)
				end
				Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(p)
					p.Chatted:Connect(function(msg) onChatted(p,msg) end)
				end)
				privateProperties.Text = "{SPY "..(enabled and "EN" or "DIS").."ABLED}"
				StarterGui:SetCore("ChatMakeSystemMessage",privateProperties)
				local chatFrame = player.PlayerGui.Chat.Frame
				chatFrame.ChatChannelParentFrame.Visible = true
				chatFrame.ChatBarParentFrame.Position = chatFrame.ChatChannelParentFrame.Position+UDim2.new(UDim.new(),chatFrame.ChatChannelParentFrame.Size.Y)
				--Credit to O Plays on Youtube, go subscribe to him (not my account, just advertising for him, we don't even know eachother lol)
			end

			if arg1 == "betterlight" then
				setstate("betterlight", arg2)

				if states.BETTERLIGHT == true then
					game.Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(70,70,70)
					game.Lighting.Brightness = 3
					game.Lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)
					game.Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 0.343
					game.Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)
					game.Lighting.ShadowSoftness = 0.2
					game.Lighting.ExposureCompensation = 0.34
					atmos = Instance.new("Atmosphere",game.Lighting)
					bloom = Instance.new("BloomEffect",game.Lighting)
					colorco = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect",game.Lighting)
					sunrays = Instance.new("SunRaysEffect",game.Lighting)

					atmos.Density = 0.2
					atmos.Offset = 0.25
					atmos.Color = Color3.fromRGB(199,199,199)
					atmos.Decay = Color3.fromRGB(106,112,125)
					atmos.Glare = 0
					atmos.Haze = 0

					bloom.Intensity = 0.5
					bloom.Size = 5
					bloom.Threshold = 0.5

					colorco.Brightness = 0.1
					colorco.Contrast = 0
					colorco.Saturation = 0.6
					colorco.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

					sunrays.Intensity = 0.117
					sunrays.Spread = 1
				end

					game.Lighting.Ambient = oldAmbien
					game.Lighting.Brightness = oldBri
					game.Lighting.ColorShift_Top = oldColorsh
					game.Lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = oldEv
					game.Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = oldOA
					game.Lighting.ShadowSoftness = oldSs
					game.Lighting.ExposureCompensation = oldex

						atmos:Destroy()
						bloom:Destroy()
						colorco:Destroy()
						sunrays:Destroy()
					end
				end

			if arg1 == "cape" then
				setstate("CAPE", arg2)
				cape()
			end

			if arg1 == "capecolor" then
				if tonumber(arg2) and tonumber(arg3) and tonumber(arg4) then
					capeColor = Color3.fromRGB(arg2, arg3, arg4)
					Notify("New cape color: "..arg2.." "..arg3.." "..arg4)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "capematerial" then
				if arg2 then
					Material = GetNameFromList(arg2, allMaterials)
					if Material then
						capeMaterial = Enum.Material[Material]
						Notify("New material: "..Material)
						respawn()
					end
				end
			end

			-- ANTIABUSERS COMMANDS

			if arg1 == "crim2" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then
					local savedpos = GetRO()
					local savedteam = game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor.Color
					local get = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
					local stop = 0
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Name = 1
				    local l = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["1"]:Clone()
				    l.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				    l.Name = "Humanoid"
				    wait(0.1)
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["1"]:Destroy()
				    game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
					repeat wait()
						stop = stop + 1
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = get.CFrame
						spawnlocations[4].CFrame = get.CFrame
						spawnlocations[4].Transparency = 1
						spawnlocations[4].CanCollide = false

						pcall(function()
							if workspace:FindFirstChild(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and ((game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Part').Position-workspace[player.Name]:FindFirstChildOfClass('Part').Position).magnitude < 10) and player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer then
								for i = 1,workspace[player.Name].Humanoid.Health/5 do
									game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").meleeEvent:FireServer(player)
								end
							end
						end)
					until (not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart or not get or not get.Parent or player.TeamColor.Name == "Really red" or stop > 100)
					wait()
					spawnlocations[4].CFrame = CFrame.new(778, 500, 2465)
	                spawnlocations[4].AllowTeamChangeOnTouch = false
					wait(0.5)
					refreshTeam(savedteam)
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedpos
					
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "antibringnoroot" or arg1 == "abnoroot" or arg1 == "abnr" then
				setstate("ANTIBRING_NO_ROOT", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "ab" or arg1 == "antibring" then
				setstate("ANTIBRING", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "avoidbring" or arg1 == "avb" then
				setstate("AVOIDBRING", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "annoy" then
                local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
			    if player then
				   states.ANNOY = player
				else
					if arg2 == "off" or not arg2 then
						states.ANNOY = nil
					end
			    end
			end

			if arg1 == "loopcopyteam" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then
					states.LOOP_COPY_TEAM = player
				else
					if arg2 == "off" then
						states.LOOP_COPY_TEAM = nil
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "loopcrim" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then
					states.LOOP_CRIM = player
				else
					if arg2 == "off" or not arg2 then
						states.LOOP_CRIM = nil
						wait(0.5)
						spawnlocations[3].CFrame = CFrame.new(778, 500, 2465)
	                    spawnlocations[3].AllowTeamChangeOnTouch = false
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "looptp" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then
					states.LOOP_TP = player
				else
					if arg2 == "off" or not arg2 then
						states.LOOP_TP = nil
					end
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "antiinvis" then
				setstate("anti_invisible", arg2)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "antifling" then
				setstate("ANTIFLING", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "on" then
				setstate("ANTICRIM", arg1, true)
				setstate("ANTISHIELD", arg1, true)
				setstate("AUTOGUNS", arg1, true)
				setstate("AUTORESPAWN", arg1, true)
				setstate("AUTOLOCK", arg1, true)
				setstate("ANTI_SPAM_ARREST_LAG", arg1, true)
				setstate("ANTIARMORSPAM", arg1, true)
				Notify("STATES enabled", green)
				coroutine.wrap(function()
					if states.AUTOLOCK == true then
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 24
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.ClientInputHandler.Disabled = true
					end
				end)()
				coroutine.wrap(function()
					getGans()
				end)()
			end

			if arg1 == "off" then
				setstate("ANTICRIM", arg1, true)
				setstate("ANTISHIELD", arg1, true)
				setstate("AUTOGUNS", arg1, true)
				setstate("AUTORESPAWN", arg1, true)
				setstate("AUTOLOCK", arg1, true)
				setstate("ANTI_SPAM_ARREST_LAG", arg1, true)
				setstate("ANTIARMORSPAM", arg1, true)
				Notify("STATES disabled", red)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "antiarmorspam" then
				setstate("antiarmorspam", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "fastpunch" or arg1 == "fp" then
				setstate("FAST_PUNCH", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "armorspam" then
				setstate("ARMOR_SPAM", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "ts" or arg1 == "timestop" then
				while wait() do
					coroutine.wrap(function()
						pcall(function()
							workspace.Remote.ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver["Remington 870"].ITEMPICKUP)

							local Gun = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack["Remington 870"] or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["Remington 870"]

							local args = {
								[1] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [2] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [3] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [4] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [5] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [6] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [7] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [8] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [9] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [10] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [11] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [12] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [13] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [14] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [15] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [16] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [17] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [18] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [19] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [20] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [21] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [22] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [23] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [24] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge,
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}, [25] = {
									["RayObject"] = Ray.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()), 
									["Distance"] = math.huge, 
									["Cframe"] = CFrame.new(), 
									["Hit"] = workspace[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name].Head
								}
							}

							game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ShootEvent:FireServer(args, Gun)
						end)
					end)()
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "anticrash" then
				setstate("ANTICRASH", arg2)
				wait()
				if states.ANTICRASH == true then
					for i,v in pairs(getconnections(game.ReplicatedStorage.ReplicateEvent.OnClientEvent)) do
						v:Disable()
					end
				else
					for i,v in pairs(getconnections(game.ReplicatedStorage.ReplicateEvent.OnClientEvent)) do
						v:Enable()
					end
				end	
			end

			if arg1 == "end" then
				Notify("Ending server")
				local PackageSize = 100000
				local SendPackageAmountOfTimes = 5

				local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
				local Players = game:GetService("Players")
				local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

				local ItemHandler = workspace:WaitForChild("Remote").ItemHandler
				local ShootEvent = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("ShootEvent")

				ItemHandler:InvokeServer(workspace.Prison_ITEMS.giver["Remington 870"].ITEMPICKUP)
				local Tool = Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild("Remington 870") or workspace:WaitForChild(Players.LocalPlayer.Name):FindFirstChild("Remington 870")

				local Packet = {
					RayObject = Ray.new(Vector3.new(-1, -1, -1), Vector3.new(1, 1, 1)),
					Distance = math.huge,
					Cframe = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0),
					Hit = workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Part")
				}

				local Package = {}

				for i = 1, PackageSize do
					Package[i] = Packet
				end

				for i = 1, SendPackageAmountOfTimes do
					ShootEvent:FireServer(Package, Tool)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "god" then
				setstate("GOD_MODE", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "to" or arg1 == "goto" then
				player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
				if player then 
					local char = workspace:FindFirstChild(player.Name)
					local hum = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					local head = char and char:FindFirstChild("Head")
			
					local m_char = workspace:FindFirstChild(UserName)
					local m_hum = m_char and m_char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					if m_char and m_hum and char and (char or head) then 
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = hum and hum.CFrame or head.CFrame
					end
					Notify("Teleported to "..player.Name, green)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "anticrim" then
				setstate("anticrim", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "antiteams" then
				setstate("antiteams", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "arrestaura" then
				setstate("arrest_aura", arg2)
			end

			if arg1 == "arrest" then
				arrest2(GetPlayerFromString(arg2))
			end
			
			if arg1 == "bring" or arg1 == "get" then
				teleport(GetPlayerFromString(arg2), game.Players.LocalPlayer)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "crim" then
				teleportCrim(GetPlayerFromString(arg2), game.Players.LocalPlayer)
			end

			if arg1 == "view" then
				local player = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)

				if player ~= nil then
					states.VIEWING = player
					Notify("Viewing "..player.Name, green)
				end
			end

			if arg1 == "unview" then
				states.VIEWING = nil
				workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				Notify("Unviewing", red)
			end

            if arg1 == "sa" or arg1 == "spamarrest" then
				if arg2 then
					if arg2 == "off" then
						states.SPAM_ARRESTING = nil
						Notify("Spam arresting: OFF", red)
					else
						states.GOD_MODE = true
						states.ANTITEAMS = true
						states.SPAM_ARRESTING = GetPlayerFromString(arg2)
						Notify("Spam arresting: "..GetPlayerFromString(arg2).Name.." @"..GetPlayerFromString(arg2).DisplayName, green)
					end
				end
            end
			
			if arg1 == "kill" or arg1 == "k" then
				if arg2 == "all" then
					Notify("Killed all")
					
					for i,v in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
						kill1(v, true)
					end
				else
					kill1(GetPlayerFromString(arg2))
				end
			end
			
			if arg1 == "loopkill" or arg1 == "lk" then
				loopkill(arg2)
			end
			
			if arg1 == "unloopkill" or arg1 == "unlk" then
				unloopkill(arg2)
			end

			-- ANTILAG COMMANDS
			if arg1 == "antisalag" then
				setstate("ANTI_SPAM_ARREST_LAG", arg2)
			end
		end
	end
	
	do_command()
end

-- ADMIN CHAT
