	get_command(true, msg)
end)

-- GIVE-ADMIN

-- UI SCRIPTING

local cmdopenpos = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.94040513, 0)
local cmdclosepos = UDim2.new(-0.192, 0, 0.94040513, 0)

local commandsopenpos = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.730631649, 0)
local commandclosepos = UDim2.new(-0.192, 0, 0.730631649, 0)

UIS.InputBegan:connect(function(input, process)
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
		if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Return and states.CMDBAR == true then
			get_command(false)
			wait(0.03)
			TextBox.Text = " "
		end
	end
end)

UIS.InputBegan:connect(function(input, process)
	if process or ADMINLOADED == false then return end
	-- CMD Bar
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Period then
		if states.CMDBAR == true then
			script.Disabled = true
			CmdBar:TweenPosition(
				cmdclosepos,
				Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
				Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
				0.3,
				true
			)
			
			wait(0.5)
			states.CMDBAR = false
			script.Disabled = false	
			wait(0.3)
			TextBox.Text = " "
		else
			script.Disabled = true
			CmdBar:TweenPosition(
				cmdopenpos,
				Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
				Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
				0.3,
				true
			)

			wait(0.5)
			
			states.CMDBAR = true
			TextBox:CaptureFocus()
			script.Disabled = false	
		end
	end
	
	-- Commands
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.K then
		if states.COMMANDS == true then
			script.Disabled = true
			CmdList:TweenPosition(
				commandclosepos,
				Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
				Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
				0.3,
				true
			)
			
			wait(0.3)
			states.COMMANDS = false
			script.Disabled = false	
		else
			script.Disabled = true
			CmdList:TweenPosition(
				commandsopenpos,
				Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
				Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
				0.3,
				true
			)

			wait(0.3)
			states.COMMANDS = true
			script.Disabled = false		
		end
	end
	-- Output
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.P then
		if Output.Visible == true then
			Output.Visible = false
		else
			Output.Visible = true
		end
	end
end)

TextBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
	script.Disabled = true
	CmdBar:TweenPosition(
		cmdclosepos,
		Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
		Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
		0.3,
		true
	)

	wait(0.5)
	states.CMDBAR = false
	script.Disabled = false	
	wait(0.3)
	TextBox.Text = " "
end)

function IsEven(num)
	return num % 2 == 0
end

longestText = 0

for i,v in pairs(allcmds) do
	clone = singlecmd:Clone()
	clone.Parent = Scrolling
	clone.Text = singlecmd.Text..v
	textSize = game:GetService("TextService"):GetTextSize(singlecmd.Text..v,singlecmd.TextSize,singlecmd.Font,singlecmd.AbsoluteSize)
	if textSize.X > longestText then
		longestText = textSize.X
	end
	clone.LayoutOrder = i
end

Scrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,longestText,0,TextLabel.TextSize * #allcmds)

-- LOOPS/AUTOMATICS/KEYBINDS

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if states.COLOR_GUNS == true then
			pcall(function()
				local backpack = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
				local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				--REMINGTON
				local rem = backpack:FindFirstChild("Remington 870") or character:FindFirstChild("Remington 870")
				if rem then
					for i,part in pairs(rem.Model:GetChildren()) do
						part.Color = colorforguns
					end
				end
			end)
			pcall(function()
				local backpack = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
				local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				-- AK-47
				local ak = backpack:FindFirstChild("AK-47") or character:FindFirstChild("AK-47")
				if ak then
					for i,part in pairs(ak.Model:GetChildren()) do
						part.Color = colorforguns
					end
				end
			end)
			pcall(function()
				local backpack = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
				local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				-- M4A1
				local m4 = backpack:FindFirstChild("M4A1") or character:FindFirstChild("M4A1")
				if m4 then
					for i,part in pairs(m4.Model:GetChildren()) do
						part.Color = colorforguns
					end
				end
			end)
			pcall(function()
				local backpack = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
				local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				-- M9
				local m9 = backpack:FindFirstChild("M9") or character:FindFirstChild("M9")
				if m9 then
					m9.Part.Color = colorforguns
				end
			end)
		end
	end
	
end)()

-- GOD MODE

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if states.GOD_MODE == true then
			pcall(function()
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Name = 1
				local l = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["1"]:Clone()
				l.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				l.Name = "Humanoid"
				wait()
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["1"]:Destroy()
				game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterRemoving:Wait()
				local savedcf = GetPos()
				local savedcamcf = GetCamPos()
				local savedteam = GetTeam()
				workspace.Remote.loadchar:InvokeServer(nil, BrickColor.new(savedteam).Name)
				workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame = savedcamcf
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = savedcf
			end)
		end
	end
end)()

	game:GetService("RunService").Stepped:connect(function()

					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Name = 1
				    local l = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["1"]:Clone()

				    l.Name = "Humanoid"
				    wait()
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["1"]:Destroy()
			        game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
				    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = "None"
				end
			end
		end
	end)
end)()

-- ANTI-SHIELD

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		for _,player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer then
				if states.ANTISHIELD == true then
					pcall(function()
						if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild(player.Name).Torso:FindFirstChild("ShieldFolder") then
							game.Workspace:FindFirstChild(player.Name).Torso:FindFirstChild("ShieldFolder"):Destroy()
						end
					end)
				end
				if states.ANTISHIELD == true then
					pcall(function()
						if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild(player.Name):FindFirstChild("Riot Shield") then
							game.Workspace:FindFirstChild(player.Name):FindFirstChild("Riot Shield"):Destroy()
						end
					end)
				end
			end
		end
	end
end)()

-- SPAM ARREST
coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait(0.03) do
		if states.SPAM_ARRESTING ~= nil then
			pcall(function()
				if states.SPAM_ARRESTING.TeamColor.Name == "Bright orange" then
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(917, 78, 2389)
					teleport(states.SPAM_ARRESTING, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
				else
					if states.SPAM_ARRESTING.TeamColor.Name ~= "Really red" then
						criminpos(states.SPAM_ARRESTING)
					end
				end
			end)
		end
	end
end)()

end)()

coroutine.wrap(function()

				local hum = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				local head = char and char:FindFirstChild("Head")
		
				local m_char = workspace:FindFirstChild(UserName)
				local m_hum = m_char and m_char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if m_char and m_hum and char and (char or head) then 
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = hum and hum.CFrame or head.CFrame
				end
			end)
		end
	end
end)()

-- LOOPCRIM

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if states.LOOP_CRIM ~= nil then
			pcall(function()
				local char = workspace:FindFirstChild(states.LOOP_CRIM.Name)
				local hum = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				local head = char and char:FindFirstChild("Head")
	
				local m_char = workspace:FindFirstChild(UserName)
				local m_hum = m_char and m_char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if m_char and m_hum and char and (char or head) then 
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = hum and hum.CFrame or head.CFrame
				end


				local crim = spawnlocations[3]
				crim.CanCollide = false
				crim.CFrame = GetRO()
				crim.Transparency = 1
			end)
		end
	end
end)()

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if states.INFINITE_AMMO == true then
			pcall(function()
				for _,v in pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
					if v:FindFirstChild("GunStates") then
						local gun = require(v.GunStates)
						gun["MaxAmmo"] = math.huge
						gun["StoredAmmo"] = math.huge
						gun["AmmoPerClip"] = math.huge
						gun["CurrentAmmo"] = math.huge
						gun["ReloadTime"] = 0
					end
				end
			end)
		end
	end

end)()

-- PLAYER JOINS/LEFTS
game.Players.PlayerAdded:connect(function(plr)
	local displayname = " @"..plr.DisplayName
	if plr.Name == plr.DisplayName then
		displayname = ""
	end

	if checkBlacklist(plr) == true or checkDisplayBlackList(plr) == true then
		states.SPAM_ARRESTING = plr
		Blacklist(plr.Name..displayname.." is an abusive and enlisted exploiter.")
	end

	if states.PLAYER_NOTIFICATIONS == true then
		if plr.AccountAge < 80 then
			Warning(plr.Name..displayname.." it's a possible alt: "..plr.AccountAge)
		else
			positiveNotify(plr.Name..displayname.." joined the game.")
		end
	end
end)

game.Players.PlayerRemoving:connect(function(plr)
	local displayname = " @"..plr.DisplayName
	if plr.Name == plr.DisplayName then
		displayname = ""
	end

	if states.PLAYER_NOTIFICATIONS == true then
		negativeNotify(plr.Name..displayname.." left the game.")
		if states.SPAM_ARRESTING == plr then
			states.SPAM_ARRESTING = nil
		end
		removeplayer(plr, friends)
		removeplayer(plr, loopkills)
	end
end)

-- FadeFrame FPS UNLOCKER GLITCH

game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui"):WaitForChild("Home").intro.Content.menus.teamsGui.Guards.Button.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	local players = GetPlayersInTeam("Guards")
	if #players > 7 then return end
	tweenservice:Create(FadeFrameFake, TweenInfo.new(1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
	wait(1)
	tweenservice:Create(FadeFrameFake, TweenInfo.new(1), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
end)

game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui"):WaitForChild("Home").intro.Content.menus.teamsGui.Prisoners.Button.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	tweenservice:Create(FadeFrameFake, TweenInfo.new(1), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
	wait(1)
	tweenservice:Create(FadeFrameFake, TweenInfo.new(1), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
end)

game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui"):WaitForChild("Home").hud.MenuButton.MenuFrame.respawn.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
	tweenservice:Create(FadeFrameFake, TweenInfo.new(0.7), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
	wait(1)
	tweenservice:Create(FadeFrameFake, TweenInfo.new(0.7), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
end)



-- ENDING SCRIPT

wait(1)
Notify("Welcome to GHXST Admin", green)
ADMINLOADED = true
